CREATE TABLE matches (match_id INT PRIMARY KEY, match_date DATE, team1_id INT, team2_id INT, winner_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (team1_id) REFERENCES teams(team_id), FOREIGN KEY (team2_id) REFERENCES teams(team_id), FOREIGN KEY (winner_id) REFERENCES teams(team_id));</t><s>UPSERT INTO matches (match_id, match_date, team1_id, team2_id, winner_id) VALUES (1, '2023-01-01', 1, 2, 1) ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE match_date = '2023-01-01', team1_id = 1, team2_id = 2, winner_id = 1;</s>

<t>CREATE TABLE team (team_id INT PRIMARY KEY, team_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, sport VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL)

CREATE TABLE player (player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, team_id INT NOT NULL, age INT) REFERENCES team(team_id)

CREATE TABLE match (match_id INT PRIMARY KEY, match_date DATE NOT NULL, team1_id INT NOT NULL, team2_id INT NOT NULL) REFERENCES team(team_id)

CREATE TABLE stadium (stadium_id INT PRIMARY KEY, stadium_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, city VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL)

CREATE TABLE tournament (tournament_id INT PRIMARY KEY, tournament_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, sport VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL)</t><s>INSERT INTO team (team_id, team_name, sport) VALUES (1, 'Team A', 'Football') ON CONFLICT (team_id) DO UPDATE SET team_name = 'Team A', sport = 'Football';</s>

CREATE TABLE stadium (stadium_id INT PRIMARY KEY, stadium_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, city VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL)

CREATE TABLE match (match_id INT PRIMARY KEY, match_date DATE NOT NULL, team1_id INT NOT NULL, team2_id INT NOT NULL) REFERENCES team(team_id)</t><s>INSERT INTO player (player_id, player_name, team_id, age) VALUES (1, 'Player 1', 1, 25) ON CONFLICT (player_id) DO UPDATE SET player_name = 'Player 1', team_id = 1, age = 25;</s>

CREATE TABLE stadium (stadium_id INT PRIMARY KEY, stadium_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, city VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL)

CREATE TABLE player (player_id INT PRIMARY KEY, player_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, team_id INT NOT NULL, age INT) REFERENCES team(team_id)

CREATE TABLE tournament (tournament_id INT PRIMARY KEY, tournament_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, sport VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL)</t><s>INSERT INTO match (match_id, match_date, team1_id, team2_id) VALUES (1, '2022-01-20', 1, 2) ON CONFLICT (match_id) DO UPDATE SET match_date = '2022-01-20', team1_id = 1, team2_id = 2;</s>
